           <div id="entries">
            <div class="entry post clearfix">
             <div class="social-wrap" style="margin-bottom:30px;float:right;margin-right:45px;padding-left:20px;">
              <a class="share-facebook share-icon" href="https://designerglassmosaics.com/fireplace/dogwood-irises-mosaic-fireplace-surround/?share=facebook&amp;nb=1" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="Share on Facebook">
               <img src="http://designerglassmosaics.com/wordpress/wp-content/themes/Aggregate/images/facebook-share-buttons.jpg"/>
              </a>
              <div style="display:inline;margin-left:15px;">
               <a class="pin-it-btn" href="javascript:void(0)" title="Pin It on Pinterest">
               </a>
              </div>

             <h1 class="title">
              Mosaic Fireplace Surround/Dogwood and Irises
             </h1>
             <div class="pin-it-btn-wrapper">
              <a data-pin-color="white" data-pin-config="beside" data-pin-do="buttonBookmark" data-pin-height="28" href="//www.pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdesignerglassmosaics.com%2Ffireplace%2Fdogwood-irises-mosaic-fireplace-surround%2F&amp;media=http%3A%2F%2Fdesignerglassmosaics.com%2Fgallery%2Ffireplace-surround-Scowden6.jpg&amp;description=Mosaic%20Fireplace%20Surround%2FDogwood%20and%20Irises" rel="nobox">
               <img alt="" button="true" src="//assets.pinterest.com/images/pidgets/pin_it_button.png" title=""/>
              </a>
             </div>
             <div class="dgmDisplayGrid clearfix">
              <a class="grouped_elements" href="https://designerglassmosaics.com/gallery/fireplace-surround-Scowden6.jpg" rel="group1">
               <img alt="" class="headImg" src="https://designerglassmosaics.com/gallery/fireplace-surround-Scowden6.jpg" width="554"/>
              </a>
              <br/>
              <a class="grouped_elements" href="https://designerglassmosaics.com/gallery/backsplash-seascape1.jpg" rel="group1">
               <img alt="" class="gridImgLeft" src="https://designerglassmosaics.com/gallery/Fireplace-surround-Scowden5.jpg" width="272"/>
              </a>
              <br/>
              <a class="grouped_elements" href="https://designerglassmosaics.com/gallery/Fireplace-surround-Scowden1.jpg" rel="group1">
               <img alt="" class="gridTbTop" src="https://designerglassmosaics.com/gallery/Fireplace-surround-Scowden1.jpg" width="272"/>
              </a>
             </div>
             <p>
              Mosaic Fireplace Surround in theme of Dogwood branch and Irises
             </p>
             <p>
              For this commissioned mosaic project we started with a design sketch prepared by the client (see photo above). Saundra, our design coordinator, next translated this design to the backerboard panels in pencil and our team of mosaic artisans hand-cut the colorful glass shapes to fit. The panels were pre-grouted in our design center. We also provided the fused glass tiles outlining the border of the fire box.
             </p>
             <p>
              Installed in New York
             </p>
             <p style="font-weight: 900;">
              Pricing depends upon the complexity of design and size of the glass artwork. Please
              <a href="http://designerglassmosaics.com/contact/" target="_contact">
               contact us
              </a>
              for specific pricing for your project.  Please call our design coordinator Saundra at 704-488-5800 to discuss your project ideas, design, colors, general pricing, etc.
             </p>
             <div class="social-wrap">
              <a class="share-facebook share-icon" href="https://designerglassmosaics.com/fireplace/dogwood-irises-mosaic-fireplace-surround/?share=facebook&amp;nb=1" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="Share on Facebook">
               <img src="http://designerglassmosaics.com/wordpress/wp-content/themes/Aggregate/images/facebook-share-buttons.jpg"/>
              </a>
              <div style="display:inline;margin-left:15px;">
               <a class="pin-it-btn" href="javascript:void(0)" title="Pin It on Pinterest">
               </a>
              </div>

           <script>
            jQuery(window).load(function() {
//jQuery(document).ready(function() {
	var numImgs = jQuery('.dgmDisplayGrid img').length;
	var headWidth = jQuery(".headImg").width();
	var headHeight = jQuery(".headImg").height();
	var headRatio = headWidth / headHeight;
	var dgmMagnify = 1.58;
	//alert(headRatio.toFixed(2));

	if (headRatio &lt;= 1) {
		var dgmMagnify = 1;
		jQuery(".headImg").css("margin-right","100px");
		
	} 
		if (numImgs == 1) {
		var dgmMagnify = .85;
		jQuery(".dgmDisplayGrid").css("text-align", "center");
		jQuery(".dgmDisplayGrid img").css("margin", "0 auto");
		jQuery(".dgmDisplayGrid img").css("float", "none");
	}

	jQuery(".dgmDisplayGrid").width((jQuery(".dgmDisplayGrid").width())*1.6);
	jQuery(".dgmDisplayGrid img").each(function() {
	var imageWidth = jQuery(this).width();
	var newWidth = imageWidth * dgmMagnify;

	jQuery(this).width(newWidth);
	var imageHeight = jQuery(this).height();
	var newHeight = imageHeight * dgmMagnify;
	jQuery(this).height('auto');
  });


});
           </script>

		var $portfolioItem = jQuery('.et_pt_gallery_entry');
	$portfolioItem.find('.et_pt_item_image').css('background-color','#000000');
	jQuery('.zoom-icon, .more-icon').css({'opacity':'0','visibility':'visible'});
	
	$portfolioItem.hover(function(){
		jQuery(this).find('.et_pt_item_image').stop(true, true).animate({top: -10}, 500).find('img.portfolio').stop(true, true).animate({opacity: 0.7},500);
		jQuery(this).find('.zoom-icon').stop(true, true).animate({opacity: 1, left: 65},400);
		jQuery(this).find('.more-icon').stop(true, true).animate({opacity: 1, left: 145},400);
		jQuery(this).find('.dgm-refer').stop(true, true).animate({opacity: 1, bottom: 5},400);
	}, function(){
		jQuery(this).find('.zoom-icon').stop(true, true).animate({opacity: 0, left: 40},400);
		jQuery(this).find('.more-icon').stop(true, true).animate({opacity: 0, left: 170},400);
		jQuery(this).find('.dgm-refer').stop(true, true).animate({opacity: 0, bottom: -20},400);
		jQuery(this).find('.et_pt_item_image').stop(true, true).animate({top: 0}, 500).find('img.portfolio').stop(true, true).animate({opacity: 1},500);
	});
	
		var $portfolioItem = jQuery('.et_pt_gallery_entry_portrait');
	$portfolioItem.find('.et_pt_item_image').css('background-color','#000000');
	jQuery('.zoom-icon-portrait, .more-icon-portrait').css({'opacity':'0','visibility':'visible'});
	
	$portfolioItem.hover(function(){

		jQuery(this).find('.zoom-icon-portrait').stop(true, true).animate({opacity: 1, left: 35},400);
